Scheduler Plugin Framework Architecture\\n\\nThe Kubernetes scheduler implements a sophisticated plugin framework for the scheduling cycle. Top-Level Scheduler Entry Point\\n\\n**File: `pkg/scheduler/scheduler.go`**\\n\\nThe `Scheduler` struct (line 66) represents the top-level scheduler component that manages:\\n- The scheduler cache for node/pod state\\n- The scheduling queue for pending pods\\n- Multiple scheduling profiles\\n- Event handlers for cluster changes\\n\\nThe `Run` method (line 464) is the main entry point that starts the scheduling loop. Scheduling Orchestration\\n\\n**File: `pkg/scheduler/schedule_one.go`**\\n\\nThe `ScheduleOne` function (line 65) implements the complete scheduling workflow for a single pod:\\n1. includes `ScoreExtensions` interface\\n- `ScoreExtensions` (line 598): Called for score normalization after all plugins score\\n- `ReservePlugin` (line 624): Updates plugin state when a pod is reserved (assumes the node)\\n- `PreBindPlugin` (line 640): Final checks before pod binding\\n- `PermitPlugin` (line 660): Permits or delays pod binding\\n- `BindPlugin` (line 673): Actually binds the pod to the node\\n- `PostBindPlugin` (line 649): Cleanup after successful binding\\n\\n**Framework Interfaces:**\\n- `Framework` (line 686): Main interface for scheduler plugins, embeds `Handle` and provides:\\n  - Plugin accessor methods (`PreEnqueuePlugins()`, `EnqueueExtensions()`, `QueueSortFunc()`)\\n  - Plugin runner methods (`RunPreFilterPlugins()`, `RunFilterPlugins()`, `RunScorePlugins()`, etc.)\\n  - Plugin checker methods (`HasFilterPlugins()`, `HasPostFilterPlugins()`, `HasScorePlugins()`)\\n  - Configuration methods (`ListPlugins()`, `ProfileName()`, `PercentageOfNodesToScore()`)\\n  - Lifecycle methods (`SetPodNominator()`, `SetPodActivator()`, `Close()`)\\n\\n- `Handle` (line 783): Provides data and tools for plugins, including:\\n  - Pod and node listers\\n  - Client set and informer factory access\\n  - Shared DRA Manager for dynamic resource allocation\\n  - Pod nomination tracking\\n\\n### 4. Scheduler Plugin Framework Architecture\\n\\nThe Kubernetes scheduler implements a sophisticated plugin framework for the scheduling cycle. Here are the key architectural components:\\n\\n### 1. Top-Level Scheduler Entry Point\\n\\n**File: `pkg/scheduler/scheduler.go`**\\n\\nThe `Scheduler` struct (line 66) represents the top-level scheduler component that manages:\\n- The scheduler cache for node/pod state\\n- The scheduling queue for pending pods\\n- Multiple scheduling profiles\\n- Event handlers for cluster changes\\n\\nThe `Run` method (line 464) is the main entry point that starts the scheduling loop. It initializes the scheduling queue and launches a goroutine that continuously calls `ScheduleOne` in a loop via `wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, sched.ScheduleOne, 0)`.\\n\\n### 2. Scheduling Orchestration\\n\\n**File: `pkg/scheduler/schedule_one.go`**\\n\\nThe `ScheduleOne` function (line 65) implements the complete scheduling workflow for a single pod:\\n1. Gets the next pod from the scheduling queue\\n2. Finds the appropriate scheduling profile for the pod\\n3. Orchestrates the full plugin execution chain through the framework\\n4. Handles success (binding pod to node) and failure (triggering preemption or requeuing)\\n\\n### 3. Framework Interface Definitions\\n\\n**File: `pkg/scheduler/framework/interface.go`**\\n\\nDefines all plugin interfaces and the Framework abstraction:\\n\\n**Core Plugin Interfaces by Extension Point:**\\n- `Plugin` (line 443): Base interface all plugins must implement with `Name()` method\\n- `PreEnqueuePlugin` (line 452): Called before pods are added to the active queue\\n- `QueueSortPlugin` (line 464): Determines pod ordering in the scheduling queue\\n- `EnqueueExtensions` (line 482): Allows plugins to register cluster events that affect pod scheduling\\n- `PreFilterPlugin` (line 512): Initial filtering phase, can reduce node candidates\\n- `PreFilterExtensions` (line 501): Incremental updates for PreFilter state (AddPod, RemovePod)\\n- `FilterPlugin` (line 540): Main filtering phase for feasibility checks\\n- `PostFilterPlugin` (line 561): Runs after filtering fails (used for preemption)\\n- `PreScorePlugin` (line 587): Informational phase after filtering, before scoring\\n- `ScorePlugin` (line 607): Ranks filtered nodes; includes `ScoreExtensions` interface\\n- `ScoreExtensions` (line 598): Called for score normalization after all plugins score\\n- `ReservePlugin` (line 624): Updates plugin state when a pod is reserved (assumes the node)\\n- `PreBindPlugin` (line 640): Final checks before pod binding\\n- `PermitPlugin` (line 660): Permits or delays pod binding\\n- `BindPlugin` (line 673): Actually binds the pod to the node\\n- `PostBindPlugin` (line 649): Cleanup after successful binding\\n\\n**Framework Interfaces:**\\n- `Framework` (line 686): Main interface for scheduler plugins, embeds `Handle` and provides:\\n  - Plugin accessor methods (`PreEnqueuePlugins()`, `EnqueueExtensions()`, `QueueSortFunc()`)\\n  - Plugin runner methods (`RunPreFilterPlugins()`, `RunFilterPlugins()`, `RunScorePlugins()`, etc.)\\n  - Plugin checker methods (`HasFilterPlugins()`, `HasPostFilterPlugins()`, `HasScorePlugins()`)\\n  - Configuration methods (`ListPlugins()`, `ProfileName()`, `PercentageOfNodesToScore()`)\\n  - Lifecycle methods (`SetPodNominator()`, `SetPodActivator()`, `Close()`)\\n\\n- `Handle` (line 783): Provides data and tools for plugins, including:\\n  - Pod and node listers\\n  - Client set and informer factory access\\n  - Shared DRA Manager for dynamic resource allocation\\n  - Pod nomination tracking\\n\\n### 4. Framework Runtime Implementation\\n\\n**File: `pkg/scheduler/framework/runtime/framework.go`**\\n\\nThe `frameworkImpl` struct (line 52) is the concrete implementation of the Framework interface. It:\\n- Maintains lists of all plugin types keyed by extension point\\n- Stores plugin weights for scoring\\n- Provides parallelizer for concurrent plugin execution\\n- Tracks metrics for plugin performance\\n\\n**Key Runtime Methods (Plugin Runners):**\\n- `RunPreFilterPlugins` (line 709): Executes all PreFilter plugins and handles Skip status\\n- `RunFilterPlugins` (line 872): Runs filters on a node for a pod\\n- `RunScorePlugins` (line 1112): Scores all nodes in parallel for a pod\\n- `RunPostFilterPlugins`: Runs postfilter plugins (preemption)\\n- `RunPreScorePlugins`: Runs pre-scoring plugins\\n- `RunPreBindPlugins` (line 1261): Pre-binding validation\\n- `RunBindPlugins` (line 1318): Actually binds pod to node\\n- `RunPostBindPlugins` (line 1335): Post-binding cleanup\\n- `RunPermitPlugins` (line 1251): Permit/wait for pod binding\\n- `RunReservePluginsReserve` (line 1370): Reserves node resources\\n- `RunReservePluginsUnreserve` (line 1414): Unreserves resources on failure\\n\\nThese methods:\\n1. Extract plugins from the appropriate list (preFilterPlugins, filterPlugins, etc.)\\n2. Call each plugin's corresponding method sequentially or in parallel\\n3. Aggregate results and handle error cases\\n4. Record metrics for plugin execution duration\\n\\n### 5. Plugin Registry System\\n\\n**File: `pkg/scheduler/framework/runtime/registry.go`**\\n\\nDefines the plugin registration system:\\n- `Registry` type (line 71): `map[string]PluginFactory` for all NodePorts, TaintToleration, NodeAffinity, PodTopologySpread, VolumeBinding, VolumeZone, VolumeRestrictions, NodeResources, DynamicResources, CSILimits, InterPodAffinity\\n- Score plugins: ImageLocality, InterPodAffinity, TaintToleration, NodeAffinity, NodeResources (with variants), PodTopologySpread, VolumeBinding\\n- Binding plugins: DefaultBinder\\n- Preemption plugins: DefaultPreemption\\n- Queue sort plugin: PrioritySort\\n- Other plugins: SchedulingGates\\n\\n### Extension Point Execution Order\\n\\nThe scheduling cycle follows this sequence:\\n1. **PreEnqueue**: Before adding to scheduling queue\\n2. **QueueSort**: Order pods in queue\\n3. **PreFilter**: Initial pod feasibility analysis\\n4. **Filter**: Feasibility checks per node (parallel across nodes)\\n5. **PostFilter**: Runs only if no nodes passed filter (preemption)\\n6. **PreScore**: Informational phase with filtered nodes\\n7. **Score**: Score all feasible nodes (parallel)\\n8. **Reserve**: Mark resources as reserved\\n9. **Permit**: Allow or delay binding\\n10. **PreBind**: Final pre-binding checks\\n11. **Bind**: Bind pod to node\\n12. **PostBind**: Cleanup after successful binding\\n\\nThis architecture enables:\\n- **Pluggability**: Easy addition of custom scheduling logic\\n- **Extensibility**: Multiple extension points for different concerns\\n- **Performance**: Parallel execution where appropriate\\n- **Observability**: Built-in metrics for plugin performance\\n- **Flexibility**: In-tree and out-of-tree plugin
